Hi Hrishikesh,

Thank you for your question.

The HTTP client reporting an error code of 404 suggests that the subscriber you are attempting to register has not been found in the HSS.

There are a few potential causes of this:


?         You may not have entered the subscriber information correctly into Zoiper. To verify this in Zoiper go to Settings -> Preferences. Make sure all the information is filled out as according to this article<https://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Making_your_first_call.html>. In particular the ?Auth. username? should be <username>@<domain> so in your case 6505550691 at example.com<mailto:6505550691 at example.com>. Could you check these settings and try registering again? If it still does not work could you please send me details of how you?ve configured your subscriber in Zoiper.

?         There may be issues with the connection between Homestead and your HSS. If registrations are still not working could you please send me the full Sprout logs and Homestead logs so I can verify this.

Thanks,

Andrew

Subject: [Project Clearwater] Call between two Clearwater Deployment
In-Reply-To: <CAOgshDuLDdFhoT_KtnCxXT2r=cPcESTNQv2+6nhRiJJ7+9cidQ@mail.gmail.com>
References: <CAOgshDuLDdFhoT_KtnCxXT2r=cPcESTNQv2+6nhRiJJ7+9cidQ@mail.gmail.com>
Message-ID: <BLUPR02MB4375B56FE0521366EF4346BE5EE0@BLUPR02MB437.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi Eric,

Thank you for your question.

A call between two different Clearwater deployments is an off-net call. Both have their own sets of subscribers so you can think of them as belonging to two different mobile operators.

After you have configured<http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/IBCF.html?#install-and-configure-an-ibcf> the IBCF with deployment B?s SIP trunk nodes you should use the BGCF to route calls to deployment B through this IBCF. In order to do this you would want a BGCF record like:

{
    "routes" : [
        { "name" : "Routing to B.ims",

              "domain" : "B.ims",

              "route"  :
[?sip:<ip of IBCF>:5060<sip:%3cip%20of%20IBCF%3e:5060>?]

            }
]
}

The BGCF rule you provided below would also attempt to route this call through deployment A, this would be an on-net call which doesn?t require a BGCF record. Once you have made this change run ?sudo cw-upload_bgcf_json?.

In terms of your ENUM configuration, an ENUM server is used to translate a telephone number you are calling in to a SIP URI. This means that it is not necessary if you are attempting to call a SIP URI (this is because the domain name would feature as part of the SIP URI already: sip:+1234@<deployment B>). If you are attempting to call a telephone number which is registered against deployment B you should use an ENUM rule to let the S-CSCF know to route the call off-net:

*.4.3.2.1 IN NAPTR 1 1 "u" "E2U+sip" "!(^.*$)!sip:\\1@<deployment B>!"

Once you have made this change run ?sudo cw-upload_enum_json?

You can read here<https://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/ENUM.html> for more information on how to configure ENUM.

With these rules in place you shouldn?t require any additional DNS config. Could you please try making a call with the above BGCF/ENUM rules and let me know how it goes. If calls are still not being routed in the way in which you would expect, in addition to looking at wireshark traces you can also increase the detail of the logs which are recorded on your nodes. See here<http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Troubleshooting_and_Recovery.html?highlight=log_level> for details.

Thanks,

Andrew

> Hi Hrishikesh,
>
> Thank you for your question.
>
> The HTTP client reporting an error code of 404 suggests that the
subscriber you
> are attempting to register has not been found in the HSS.
>
> There are a few potential causes of this:
>
>
> ?         You may not have entered the subscriber information correctly
into
> Zoiper. To verify this in Zoiper go to Settings -> Preferences. Make sure
all
> the information is filled out as according to this
> article<
https://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Making_your_first_call.html>.
>  In particular the ?Auth. username? should be <username>@<domain> so in
your
> case 6505550... at example.com<mailto:6505550... at example.com>. Could you
check
> these settings and try registering again? If it still does not work could
you
> please send me details of how you?ve configured your subscriber in Zoiper.
>
> ?         There may be issues with the connection between Homestead and
your
> HSS. If registrations are still not working could you please send me the
full
> Sprout logs and Homestead logs so I can verify this.
>
> Thanks,
>
> Andrew

Looks like your computer name (or hostname) is ?ellis?
This will conflict with the installation of `ellis` package.
Change your computer name to ellis-1 or otherelse will do the trick.

Hi Astha,

You are welcome for the response. In future could you please reply to the mailing list instead of replying to me directly, that way we might be able to help some people out in the future if they have a similar issue.

If the command cw-upload_shared_config is not working for you I think you must be using an old version of Project Clearwater that was released before we added shortened names for our deployment management scripts.

We have updated our documentation now but I believe one of the following commands should work on the older versions:


*         sudo /usr/share/clearwater/clearwater-config-manager/scripts/upload_shared_config

*         sudo /usr/bin/cw-upload_shared_config

If neither of the following work could you please let me know what version of Project Clearwater you are using by running the command "clearwater-version"

Thanks,

Andrew

From: Astha Sharma [mailto:astha.sharma at aricent.com]
Sent: Friday, May 12, 2017 9:50 AM

Subject: Re: 403 forbidden on registering sip over UDP


Hi Andrew,

Thanks for quick response.

I have followed following steps:
In /etc/clearwater/shared_config set or update the fields:

a.       scscf_uri=sip:scscf.<sprout_hostname>;transport=udp<sip:scscf.%3csprout_hostname%3e;transport=udp>

b.      disable_tcp_switch=Y
In /etc/clearwater/local_config set or update the field on each of your Sprout nodes:

a.       scscf_node_uri=sip:<local_ip>:5054;transport=udp<sip:%3clocal_ip%3e:5054;transport=udp>

and after that as per your suggestion, I tried to run the command "sudo cw-upload_shared_config"

From: Andrew Edmonds <Andrew.Edmonds at metaswitch.com<mailto:Andrew.Edmonds at metaswitch.com>>
Sent: 12 May 2017 13:55:11
To: Astha Sharma
Subject: RE: 403 forbidden on registering sip over UDP

Hi Astha,

Thank you for your question about UDP support.

Project Clearwater does support using SIP-over-UDP. For details on how to configure your deployment to use UDP please follow the instructions here<http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Configuring_an_Application_Server.html#sip-over-udp-configuration>.

Once you have made these changes run the command "sudo cw-upload_shared_config" and try registering again. Let me know if this resolves your issue.

Thanks,

Andrew

From ahmedaden at gmail.com  Fri May 12 20:55:09 2017
From: ahmedaden at gmail.com (Ahmed Aden)
Date: Fri, 12 May 2017 20:55:09 -0400
Subject: [Project Clearwater] /etc/clearwater/local_settings configured
 before packages install?
Message-ID: <CAEKnsabMZwOd58OK3vMB=jGbEYdO2ft7XBE8Vu0_14YM8fpTbw@mail.gmail.com>

Hello

A mailing list response indicated that /etc/clearwater/local_settings must
have the etcd_cluster=" " IP information before the specific per-node
package installations using apt-get.


Does this I can't create pre-packaged images and update the
/etc/clearwater/local_settings file during runtime?



When you install the first set of nodes in a Project Clearwater deployment,
you need to make sure that each of the nodes in the deployment has the
correct value of etcd_cluster in /etc/clearwater/local_settings. It should
be set to a comma separated list that contains the IP address of each of
the nodes in the cluster. You should put this local_config in place on each
of your nodes before installing any of the software packages using apt-get.





http://lists.projectclearwater.org/pipermail/clearwater_lists.projectclearwater.org/2016-May/002926.html

Hi Astha,

You are welcome for the response. In future could you please reply to the mailing list instead of replying to me directly, that way we might be able to help some people out in the future if they have a similar issue.

If the command cw-upload_shared_config is not working for you I think you must be using an old version of Project Clearwater that was released before we added shortened names for our deployment management scripts.

We have updated our documentation now but I believe one of the following commands should work on the older versions:


*         sudo /usr/share/clearwater/clearwater-config-manager/scripts/upload_shared_config

*         sudo /usr/bin/cw-upload_shared_config

If neither of the following work could you please let me know what version of Project Clearwater you are using by running the command "clearwater-version"

Thanks,

Andrew

From: Astha Sharma [mailto:astha.sharma at aricent.com]
Sent: Friday, May 12, 2017 9:50 AM
To: Andrew Edmonds <Andrew.Edmonds at metaswitch.com>
Subject: Re: 403 forbidden on registering sip over UDP


Hi Andrew,

Thanks for quick response.

I have followed following steps:
In /etc/clearwater/shared_config set or update the fields:

a.       scscf_uri=sip:scscf.<sprout_hostname>;transport=udp<sip:scscf.%3csprout_hostname%3e;transport=udp>

b.      disable_tcp_switch=Y
In /etc/clearwater/local_config set or update the field on each of your Sprout nodes:

a.       scscf_node_uri=sip:<local_ip>:5054;transport=udp<sip:%3clocal_ip%3e:5054;transport=udp>

and after that as per your suggestion, I tried to run the command "sudo cw-upload_shared_config"
But it is failing:
[cw-aio]root at cw-aio:/etc/clearwater# cw-upload_shared_config
cw-upload_shared_config: command not found


Regards,
Astha

From: Andrew Edmonds <Andrew.Edmonds at metaswitch.com<mailto:Andrew.Edmonds at metaswitch.com>>
Sent: 12 May 2017 13:55:11
To: Astha Sharma
Subject: RE: 403 forbidden on registering sip over UDP

Hi Astha,

Thank you for your question about UDP support.

Project Clearwater does support using SIP-over-UDP. For details on how to configure your deployment to use UDP please follow the instructions here<http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Configuring_an_Application_Server.html#sip-over-udp-configuration>.

Once you have made these changes run the command "sudo cw-upload_shared_config" and try registering again. Let me know if this resolves your issue.

Thanks,

Andrew

From Ying.Huang at metaswitch.com  Mon May 15 05:44:18 2017
From: Ying.Huang at metaswitch.com (Ying Huang)
Date: Mon, 15 May 2017 09:44:18 +0000
Subject: [Project Clearwater] Release Note for Ecthelion
Message-ID: <DM5PR02MB24750A4C93C740164C7CBCE2F8E10@DM5PR02MB2475.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi all,

The release for Project Clearwater sprint "Ecthelion" has been cut. The code for this release is tagged as release-122 in GitHub.

This release introduces the new architecture http://www.projectclearwater.org/technical/clearwater-architecture/. We recommend any existing deployments are redeployed using the new architecture. If you are using Chef to manage your deployment and want to continue using the old architecture, then you must not pull the latest Chef changes. In order to redeploy an existing Chef-managed deployment on the new architecture, you must:

1.       delete your existing deployment with knife deployment delete -E <env>

2.        pull the latest Chef changes with git pull

3.        upload the new cookbooks with:

                                  i.            knife cookbook upload clearwater -o cookbooks/

                                 ii.            find roles/*.rb -exec knife role from file {} \;

4.        recreate your deployment as documented on http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Automated_Install.html


Issues fixed:

*         Sprout crashes when you try calling a barred subscriber who has been deregistered by an RTR

*         Sprout can generate a reg-event NOTIFY with empty XML

*         Docs are inconsistent about whether clearwater-cluster-manager is installed on all nodes

*         Chronos timers fail to pop due to unconfigured signalling DNS server

*         sprout_chronos_callback_uri breaks Sprout

*         Console spam in sprout UTs


To upgrade to this release, follow the instructions at http://docs.projectclearwater.org/en/stable/Upgrading_a_Clearwater_deployment.html.  If you are deploying an all-in-one node, the standard image (http://vm-images.cw-ngv.com/cw-aio.ova) has been updated for this release.

Ying

 before packages install?
In-Reply-To: <CAEKnsabMZwOd58OK3vMB=jGbEYdO2ft7XBE8Vu0_14YM8fpTbw@mail.gmail.com>

Message-ID: <BLUPR02MB437E66127EC170322D909CAE5E50@BLUPR02MB437.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi Ahmed,

Thank you for your question.

The file containing the etcd_cluster config setting is /etc/clearwater/local_config (not /etc/clearwater/local_settings).

We don?t have a documented process to produce pre-packaged images for our open source produce Project Clearwater. However our commercial product Clearwater Core<http://www.metaswitch.com/clearwater-ims-core> does have pre-packaged images.

As an alternative you could also download our all-in-one (AIO) OVF, for more details on this please visit here<http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/All_in_one_OVF_Installation.html>.

Andrew

From: Clearwater [mailto:clearwater-bounces at lists.projectclearwater.org] On Behalf Of Ahmed Aden
Sent: Saturday, May 13, 2017 1:55 AM
To: clearwater at lists.projectclearwater.org
Subject: [Project Clearwater] /etc/clearwater/local_settings configured before packages install?

Hello

A mailing list response indicated that /etc/clearwater/local_settings must have the etcd_cluster=" " IP information before the specific per-node package installations using apt-get.

Does this I can't create pre-packaged images and update the /etc/clearwater/local_settings file during runtime?

When you install the first set of nodes in a Project Clearwater deployment, you need to make sure that each of the nodes in the deployment has the correct value of etcd_cluster in /etc/clearwater/local_settings. It should be set to a comma separated list that contains the IP address of each of the nodes in the cluster. You should put this local_config in place on each of your nodes before installing any of the software packages using apt-get.


http://lists.projectclearwater.org/pipermail/clearwater_lists.projectclearwater.org/2016-May/002926.html

-----Original Message-----
From: Andrew Edmonds 
Sent: Friday, May 19, 2017 9:56 AM
To: 'Astha Sharma' <astha.sharma at aricent.com>
Subject: RE: Clearwater Digest, Vol 49, Issue 8

Hi Astha,

Thank you for your question.

I can see from your shared config that the parameters in the angle brackets have not been filled in correctly, in scscf_uri "<sprout_hostname>" should be replaced by the hostname of the AIO node (which you should be able to find in /etc/hostname) likewise in scscf_node "<local_ip>" should be replaced with the IP address of your AIO node (which can be found by running the command ifconfig).

Once you have done this can you please reboot the node and try making the call again. Note that the call may not work, looking through you logs I can see:

12-05-2017 23:40:46.123 UTC Debug bono.cpp:2776: Adding a Route header to sip:scscf.cw-aio:5052;transport=TCP

which suggests that Bono is sending a message to Sprout over TCP. This may still be the case after you've changed the config. However we should be able to get more helpful diagnostics once you have the correct config in place.

Thanks,

Andrew

Hi Astha,

You are welcome for the response. In future could you please reply to the mailing list instead of replying to me directly, that way we might be able to help some people out in the future if they have a similar issue.

If the command cw-upload_shared_config is not working for you I think you must be using an old version of Project Clearwater that was released before we added shortened names for our deployment management scripts.

We have updated our documentation now but I believe one of the following commands should work on the older versions:


*         sudo /usr/share/clearwater/clearwater-config-manager/scripts/upload_shared_config

*         sudo /usr/bin/cw-upload_shared_config

If neither of the following work could you please let me know what version of Project Clearwater you are using by running the command "clearwater-version"

Thanks,

Andrew

From: Andrew Edmonds <Andrew.Edmonds at metaswitch.com<mailto:Andrew.Edmonds at metaswitch.com>>
Sent: 12 May 2017 13:55:11
To: Astha Sharma
Subject: RE: 403 forbidden on registering sip over UDP

Hi Astha,

Thank you for your question about UDP support.

Project Clearwater does support using SIP-over-UDP. For details on how to configure your deployment to use UDP please follow the instructions here<http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Configuring_an_Application_Server.html#sip-over-udp-configuration>.

Once you have made these changes run the command "sudo cw-upload_shared_config" and try registering again. Let me know if this resolves your issue.

Thanks,

Andrew

Message-ID: <BLUPR02MB4370CC2D52E1A0050BC6A66E5E50@BLUPR02MB437.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

Hi Hrishikesh,

Thank you for your question.

If you look at the manual installation instructions<http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Manual_Install.html?highlight=apt%20Ellis> you can see that we instruct users to install Ellis by running the following commands:

sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive apt-get install ellis --yes
sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive apt-get install clearwater-management --yes

you can try installing Ellis again using the above commands.

There is, however, another issue with the installation I can see that you should resolve before trying this, if we look through the output of the apt-get command we can see:

usermod: user ellis is currently used by process 1222

this suggests that an existing process is causing a conflict which stops the installation from working. You can see what process 1222 is by running the command ?ps aux | grep 1222?, depending on what the process is you may be able to safely kill it and retry the installation. If there is no longer a process 1222 you can retry the installation and see if you get a similar error message for a different process ID, then you could see what that process was.

Once you have followed these steps you can retry the installation using the above commands, if the installation still does not work could you please paste me the output you get when you run the above commands.

Thanks,

Andrew

On Fri, May 19, 2017 at 3:00 PM, Andrew Edmonds <
Andrew.Edmonds at metaswitch.com> wrote:

> Hi Hrishikesh,
>
>
>
> Thank you for your question.
>
>
>
> If you look at the manual installation instructions
> <http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/Manual_Install.html?highlight=apt%20Ellis>
> you can see that we instruct users to install Ellis by running the
> following commands:
>
>
>
> sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND*=*noninteractive apt-get install ellis --yes
>
> sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive apt-get install clearwater-management
> --yes
>
>
>
> you can try installing Ellis again using the above commands.
>
>
>
> There is, however, another issue with the installation I can see that you
> should resolve before trying this, if we look through the output of the
> apt-get command we can see:
>
>
>
> usermod: user ellis is currently used by process 1222
>
>
>
> this suggests that an existing process is causing a conflict which stops
> the installation from working. You can see what process 1222 is by running
> the command ?ps aux | grep 1222?, depending on what the process is you may
> be able to safely kill it and retry the installation. If there is no longer
> a process 1222 you can retry the installation and see if you get a similar
> error message for a different process ID, then you could see what that
> process was.
>
>
>
> Once you have followed these steps you can retry the installation using
> the above commands, if the installation still does not work could you
> please paste me the output you get when you run the above commands.
>
>
>
> Thanks,
>
>
>
> Andrew
>
>
>
>

> Hi Ahmed,

>
>
> Thank you for your question.
>
>
>
> The file containing the etcd_cluster config setting is
> /etc/clearwater/local_config (not /etc/clearwater/local_settings).
>
>
>
> We don?t have a documented process to produce pre-packaged images for our
> open source produce Project Clearwater. However our commercial product Clearwater
> Core <http://www.metaswitch.com/clearwater-ims-core> does have
> pre-packaged images.
>
>
>
> As an alternative you could also download our all-in-one (AIO) OVF, for
> more details on this please visit here
> <http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/stable/All_in_one_OVF_Installation.html>
> .
>
>
>
> Andrew
>
>
>
> *From:* Clearwater [mailto:clearwater-bounces at lists.projectclearwater.org]
> *On Behalf Of *Ahmed Aden
> *Sent:* Saturday, May 13, 2017 1:55 AM
> *To:* clearwater at lists.projectclearwater.org
> *Subject:* [Project Clearwater] /etc/clearwater/local_settings configured
> before packages install?
>
>
>
> Hello
>
>
>
> A mailing list response indicated that /etc/clearwater/local_settings must
> have the etcd_cluster=" " IP information before the specific per-node
> package installations using apt-get.
>
>
>
> Does this I can't create pre-packaged images and update the
> /etc/clearwater/local_settings file during runtime?
>
>
>
> When you install the first set of nodes in a Project Clearwater
> deployment, you need to make sure that each of the nodes in the deployment
> has the correct value of etcd_cluster in /etc/clearwater/local_settings. It
> should be set to a comma separated list that contains the IP address of
> each of the nodes in the cluster. You should put this local_config in place
> on each of your nodes before installing any of the software packages using
> apt-get.
>
>
>
>
>
>
> http://lists.projectclearwater.org/pipermail/clearwater_lists.projectclearwater.org/2016-May/002926.html

>

> Clearwater mailing list
> Clearwater at lists.projectclearwater.org

From Adam.Lindley at metaswitch.com  Tue May 23 09:31:15 2017
From: Adam.Lindley at metaswitch.com (Adam Lindley)
Date: Tue, 23 May 2017 13:31:15 +0000
Subject: [Project Clearwater]  Release note for sprint Fingolfin
Message-ID: <BY2PR02MB203716706C5C0B87BB89DBC0E2F90@BY2PR02MB2037.namprd02.prod.outlook.com>

The release for Project Clearwater sprint "Fingolfin" has been cut. The code for this release is tagged as release-123 in GitHub.

This release we're upgrading etcd to the latest and greatest version.
This version isn't directly compatible with the etcd used in the previous release, so after you've upgraded all your nodes you'll need to recreate your etcd cluster following the instructions at http://clearwater.readthedocs.io/en/latest/Handling_Multiple_Failed_Nodes.html. Until you do this the etcd processes on your nodes will report failures, and you won't be able to easily upload changes to shared config or add/remove nodes.


The release also includes the following bug fixes:


*         Some calls fail if java fails on 1 of 3 vellum nodes.

*         There is no equivalent to mark_node_failed that can be used to remove a Vellum node in the other site from the Cassandra cluster

*         Queue Manager doesn't log on being stopped

*         Incorrect case for alarm severity in Sprout communication error alarms.

*         Spurious "Error impistore.cpp:664: Failed to write IMPI for private_id 5013356333 at stress.clearwater.test<mailto:5013356333 at stress.clearwater.test>" log on CAS failure

*         upload_json (and therefore all our JSON uploaders) make it easy to upload an invalid file

*         We should write better/more noticable logs on removing the data directory on etcd startup

*         Clearwater diags monitor should pull off the healthy_etcd_members file


To upgrade to this release, follow the instructions at http://docs.projectclearwater.org/en/stable/Upgrading_a_Clearwater_deployment.html.  If you are deploying an all-in-one node, the standard image (http://vm-images.cw-ngv.com/cw-aio.ova) has been updated for this release.

Adam
